       <script>
        $('.str').on('click touchstart', function (event) {
					if( $(event.target).closest(".action").length ) {
						$("input[type=radio][name='variety']").prop('checked', false);
						$("input[type=radio][value='" + $(this).attr('data-vid') + "']").prop('checked', true);
						return;
					}
					$(location).attr('href', $(this).attr('data-href'));
				});
				$('.my-collection-block').on('click touchstart', function (event) {
					if ($('#coin-list').is(":hidden")) {
						$('#coin-list').show();
						$('.my-collection-block .arrow').removeClass('abw').addClass('atw');
					} else {
						$('#coin-list').hide();
						$('.my-collection-block .arrow').removeClass('atw').addClass('abw');
					}
				});
       </script>

  <script>
   $(document).on('click touchstart', function (event) {
					if( $(event.target).closest("#avatar-popup, #notify-popup, #search-popup").length ) 
					return;
					$(".popup").fadeOut("fast");
					event.stopPropagation();
				});
				$(".popup-init").on('click touchstart', function () {
					id =  "#" + $(this).attr('data-id');
					if($(id).is(":visible")){
						$(".popup").fadeOut("fast");
					} else {
						$(".popup").fadeOut("fast");
						$(id).fadeIn("fast");
					}
					if (id == '#search-popup') {
						setTimeout(function() {
							$('#header-search-input').focus(); 
						}, 100); 
					}
					return false;
				});
				$(".popup-close").on('click touchstart', function () {
					$(".popup").fadeOut("fast");
					return false;
				});
				$("#mobile-view").on('click touchstart', function() {
					setCookie('version', 'mobile');
				});
				function setCookie(name, value) {
					var now = new Date();
					var time = now.getTime();
					var expireTime = time + 86400000 * 365 * 5; //5 Years
					now.setTime(expireTime);
					document.cookie = name+'='+value+';expires='+now.toUTCString()+';domain=ucoin.net;path=/;';
				}
  </script>
